namespace = colonize_it_e_divite
namespace = colonize_it_e_divite_menu

#分割


country_event = { #地域を選択
	id = colonize_it_e_divite.1
	title = colonize_it_e_divite.t
	desc = colonize_it_e_divite.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_region
		}
	}
	#フィルター
		option = { #次へ
			name = ci_next

			name = ci_back
			country_event = {
				id = ci_e_colonies_indexes.1
			}
		}
		option = { #交易会社地域フィルター1
			name = ci_filter_trade_company_on
			custom_tooltip = ci_filter_trade_company_on.tt
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
				country_event = {
					id = colonize_it_e_divite_copy.1
				}
			}
		}
		option = { #交易会社地域フィルター2

country_event = { #地域を選択
	id = colonize_it_e_divite_copy.1
	title = colonize_it_e_divite.t
	desc = colonize_it_e_divite.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_region
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
			set_country_flag = ci_filter_region
		}
	}
	#フィルター
		option = { #次へ
			name = ci_next

			}

			}
		}
		option = { #交易会社地域フィルター1

				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
				}

			custom_tooltip = colonize_it_e_advanced_region.tt
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
				event_target:colonize_it_target = {
					any_owned_province = {
						trade_company_region = trade_company_baltic_sea
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						trade_company_region = trade_company_baltic_sea
					}
					set_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = colonize_it_e_divite.1
				}
			}
		}

				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {

				}
			}

				has_country_flag = ci_filter_trade_company
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ci_filter_remove_mark }
				event_target:colonize_it_target = {
					any_owned_province = {
						region = carribeans_region
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						region = carribeans_region
					}
					set_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = colonize_it_e_divite.1
				}
			}
		}
